By 1975, he turned out to be right, and the doubling became immortalized as <b>Moores law.</b> Moore&#39;s law stood until 2016 when Intel suggested silicon transistors can only keep shrinking for another five years. After receiving her PhD, Ochoa co-developed three patented optical devices while at Sandia National Laboratories. Those devices would prove to have important applications for data gathering and evaluating equipment safety. In April of 1993, Ochoa traveled into space for the first time, as Mission Specialist on the STS-56 Discovery Space Shuttle Mission. In November 1994, she returned to space on Shuttle Mission STS-66 as Payload Commander. Her work on both expeditions contributed valuable information about the damage to the Earth&#39;s ozone layer.
